            <div class="fbcms_article_date">February 16, 2018</div><div class="data-driven-title fbcms_article_title">ORS Refunds to be Distributed to Current and Former Employees</div>
            <div class="fbcms_article_summary"><p>This past month, the Office of Retirement Services (ORS) provided the District with a detailed file for reimbursing the 3% health care contribution that employees had deducted from July 2010 until September 2012. By now you should have received an email from ORS that indicates the amount you contributed, the amount of accrued interest, and the total amount of your refund for each of the school districts you worked for during that period.</p>

<p><span class="content_morelink"><a href="/downloads/human_resources/3_inactive_employee_memo.pdf" target="_blank">Read the memo from Ferndale Schools for Inactive Employees</a></span>If you have any questions regarding this refund amount, please contact ORS directly at 800.381.5111.</p>
</div>

        </div>
